I have been a patient here for years between the Laguna Niguel And Newport Ofices and each time I am here I have a fantastic visit, and I always receive the very best breast diagnostic technology and high quality medical breast screening. I‚Äôm raising my opinion on The London.  4.5 Stars!

Service has always been good and definitely a 5 star rating.  The place is always busy, especially during sporting events. Of which why have like six screens covering everything.

I've tried the whole menu and can say it's getting better. Jalape√±o Burger 4.25, Mullitas 4 Stars, Chicken Sandwich 4.5 Stars, tater tots Awesome!!, garlic fries and now Breakfast!!!

The breakfast sandwich is great and they do it right. We even had the breakfast tacos.

I should mention they seem to make their own sauces. Most of them are great and the spicy one that comes with the mullitas is ridiculous. Ask for this if you want the turn up the heat.

<review>I always love discovering new places. Especially pubs. I've been to alot, so I have a pretty high standard.

First: this is a self-proclaimed gastropub. I am not 100% sure what food qualifies them to be a novelty. I've had the fish n chips. Yummy. I've had their blue cheese burger. Super yummy. I've seen their fish tacos....meh. Prices are very reasonable, but I am not seeing a signature dish.

Their beer list is decent, they actually serve Boddington's and Old Speckled Hen, which is pretty impressive. These are great draft beers.

The service for me is conflicting. They are very nice yet they are slow as molasses. A lot of business people come in for lunch, so you should time yourself to an hour. It takes too long to get your check, your refill, your order in...

This business has a lot of promise but their staff needs to step up and create that awesome experience. They also need to make good on their gastropub promise. The way I see it, it's just a nice pub.< /review><Rating>3</Rating><GmapID>0x80c2d969f4ea9b97:0x9f7ea346c9e27df6< /GmapID><pics>None<//pics><user>116534936135389243233<//user><resp>None< /resp>< date>

< text>
I've been coming here for years! My best friend swears they have the best most interesting pizzas in the Inner Richmond. I think they are okay. I will say that they definitely have unique pizza topping combinations. The beer is good, nothing crazy. Very  drinkable and priced well. They have a cool fireplace in the back too. It can be kind of confusing when you walk in because there are two sides to the restaurant, the bar side and the restaurant side. I always walk in the bar side, do a double take and then go, "yep...I need to go in the other door." They accommodated a large party for a friends birthday at last minute too. Good for a chill meal with good friends!< /text>

< Review>
My friend and I just flew in and were looking forward to trying this place.  It was around 1 PM and the place was almost empty.  We ate at the bar and the bartender Annie was incredibly friendly.  She gave us plenty of advice on what pizza and beers to try, as well as other places to visit while in San Fran (including pizza and breweries).

The beer was fresh and well balanced.  They had about 12 beers on tap, and the peach pale ale was one of my favorites there.  There pizza selection was eclectic and unique.  I had a pizza with a refried bean sauce, chicken, fresh pearl tomatoes, on top of greens and cheese; really tasty.

Overall, Pizza Orgasmica was delicious and I would recommend it to those pizza enthusiasts who want to enjoy good beer with their pizza.</Review>

< review>
Good reliable pizza and beer. My friends and I frequent the FiDi location often, so when I heard I was moving near one, I knew what would be by top go-to places for a good pie. Their thin crust pizzas are good (I save the thick crust or deep dishes for Little Star or Patxi's). They have a nice bar and lots of TVs if you wanted to just have a low-key beer and catch the game, but I have been when its gotten really loud. Having lived here for a while now, I find this location a bit strange, beautifully decorated, but not matching any of the neighboring Asian places.</review>

< rating>

<GmapID>0x8085873d99cc0635:0xfa5a9747dab26e09< /GmapID><user_id>112172538393316473174< /user_id><response>None<//response><Date>1366150962837< /Date>< review>
Pizza Orgasmica is one of the better pizzas I've ever had, but this place suffers from a lack of consistency.

First, the positives: The pizzas here are some of the most delicious, fresh, inventive pizzas I've ever had.  Highlights include the Inspiration Point (pesto, red sauce, shredded chicken, spinach, more pesto) and the Kinky Cow (red sauce, shredded carrot, ground beef, bleu cheese).  Some of the taste combinations are unusual for pizza, but they really do work.  Unlike some pizza places which throw weird stuff onto a pie and call it gourmet without caring whether the combinations play well together or taste good, this place has a good chef behind the menu.  Trust their combinations and order liberally.

Wings are a sweet asian barbecue style sauce, not the more traditional "buffalo wings" you normally find at a pizza place, and quite delicious.  The salads are great, too.

Orgasmica brews their own beers, and while they aren't the most delicious brews I've ever had, they're solid, enjoyable, and reasonably priced.  Don't be shy about ordering them.  The peach ale smells like a basket of peaches and tastes about the same.

Here's the bad part: The inconsistency. Sometimes the pizzas are perfectly done; other times they're almost burnt and they sit under the heat lamps for too long. Sometimes they're well made, with the proper balance of ingredients; other times they aren't, and you get crab meat on your chicken pizza (true story).  Sometimes the service is great and friendly; other times it's crappy and the people are rude.  It's consistent inconsistency, and it's enough to deter me from going sometimes.

It's also expensive.  $30 for an extra-large pizza?  Jebus!  Go on Tuesday nights when they have 50% off L and XL pizzas.  It's a deal then.< /review>

<user>112321323268016189314< /user><username>Christopher Calhoun (StarLord / ChrCal)< /username>< Time>

<rating>4</rating>< Text>
Beers are good. Peach ale good. Golden good. Amber good. I like beer, I brew beer. and I like drinking theirs up because they know what they are doing hehe...

Ok, Pizza is good if you like the style, its that kinda chibata bread light crust like what you get from some trader joe's pizza .. it's good, it's not omg i am going to fall on the floor and faint good, but tasty enough to keep coming back. I haven't had take out, i don't know if this would fare well as a carry out item but its fine the next day if you have leftovers. thats a good mark for pizza, shelf life, lol..

I have been here twice. that's kind of a rule now with my yelping, places i hear of and have been to more than once, but anyway,

Decor here is awesome. you are thrown back in time with the wood carvings and stained glass and mural and what not. stay in THE BAR AREA, that's where it happens. the couches and stuff are fun victorian era stuff. i could totally see a vampiress swoop in and bite my neck, leaving beer and pizza stains in her wake..

where was i.. oh yeh, try to avoid the restaurant AREA unless you have a big group of people that wouldnt otherwise fit around the bar somehow..

the restaurant had a creepy vibe like a bad feng shui sort of way, but then i am dark and jaded so maybe i was just sensing me LOL .. so far we are at a few stars...

i traditionally tip 20% seriously, like, by habit.. yes i like pizza orgasmica. i love the beer. they do have special happy hours and themed times for all sorts of fun with lower prices on stuff, but other than that, if you go during a peak time when nothing special sort of deal is going on, then, well, pirces a bit high. i had a pizza and 3 beers and think it was like 40 bucks. is that bad? uh... well $15 in beer $25 pizza? its a weeeee bit high... for one person! mmm looks like 3 stars there...  living in the city is expensive, having a bar or restaurant is too. can they lower the price or up the pizza quality somehow? this i dont have mad skillz to know.

yes theres lots of cheap shite places you can go to in the area but who has themes and brews beer and pizza? not many... not many.. worth the extra coinage? yeh.. i left happy, there was a bunch of what i gather to be USF people there getting pretty drunk and they made me laugh. i was a bit tipsy after 3 pints so good thing i can walk home from there.. ha!

that said, let me say the bartenderess is freaking cool awesome fun person major love it. dig it. nice. makes for a happy place. and she's a bit curvy which i like in a person, no stick figure tall long leg aliens with giganormous boobs out to here for me, i likes em more natural. damn, off topic again.

of the place itself, i think they have free wifi also, which is a plus.. i am going to bring a laptop sometime, plunk down in a cozy sofa, blog away while drinking beer and eating pizza. how cool is that? Ernest Hemingway would approve of the ambiance i'd suppose..

Ah you know what, I am bumping this one up from 3 to 4 stars. it's better than A-OK, I am a fan.. i'll drink and eat to that... join me there haha..< /Text>

I love this place, as a former long-term employee(5-10-18 to 5/2019 (I think the year's are right)) I can honestly say that William is a very loving and compassionate man, he's family oriented and is very positive, even when things are stressful and difficult, he keeps a smile on his face and gets what needs to be done, done. <rate>5</rate>< Text>
Amazing experience here. I brought my family of 6 in to rent bikes for the day. William took the time to outfit each of my kids (ages 4-12) with a bike that they liked. My wife and I both got cruisers.

The beach bike trail was right across the street, so we left our car there and spent the afternoon riding along the coast. Everyone had a great time.

When we returned, I liked my rental so much, that I asked William if I could buy it. He gave me a good price and  replaced the grips. I couldn't be happier with our experience there. I would recommend Rooster Wheels to anyone; large-familied or not!</Text>

Not a bad shop at all. Repairs are solid and the price is decent but turn around time is pretty long. I have had repairs done 3 times now at this shop and it has been over two week each time. < Review>
This is a really nice, clean store. I just moved to the area so I'm trying out every grocer within a half hour drive. There was a great selection of most things but my only hesitation is that there wasn't a huge selection of produce, acceptable but not amazing.  Maybe I'm mistaken but I think Vons are the same as Safeway and I know at Safeways the produce section can vary a lot by location.  The other thing I would like more selection of in an ideal world would be imports.  The international foods were very very limited. Everything they do carry was well stocked when I was there (Tuesday arvo) except a couple things people are still panic buying which is understandable. I appreciated too that there was a public toilet during covid times, a lot of places have them closed.< /Review>
